<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
Don't be intimidated by its appearance and location. This shopping center is filled with little gems like Hello Boba! You are welcomed by the busy staff, through Covid-compliant glass, wearing masks. We ordered Jasmine green tea, Royal milk tea, and the sea foam black tea. All with brown sugar boba, without extra charge. We were able to adjust the sweetness to our liking. They were allmade well, we finished them before getting back on the freeway. The boba was soft and chewy, the way they're meant to be.< /text>

<Rating>4</Rating>< Text>
I really enjoyed the Boba milk teas I ordered from here.

They are also offering Happy Hour prices during the week from Mon-Fri, 4pm-7pm (BOGO on Boba Milk Tea or Thai Milk Tea). They offer reg size (small) or bigger for $.50 more. Can't beat the HH deal, though.

I would've appreciated if they offered non-dairy milk alternatives for ALL of their drinks instead of just certain ones. Apparently, the mixes are already made so they cannot substitute/customize according to your needs.</Text>

<gmap_id>0x80c2d1db6c36bda3:0x1fdf3db0b5303a86< /gmap_id>< Review>
Newly opened Hello Boba that offers coffee, bubble tea and desserts. They are located in a small plaza by Peck rd and Garvey avenue. They have a wide variety of milk and fruit tea boba. Interior atmosphere was welcoming and  relaxing. Inside was clean, organized and spacious. Its interior decor was simple albeit cute. Some of their milk tea boba and smoothies were pretty standard however what captivated me was their fruity selection called mojito (original, mint leaves, lime, mango, peach, watermelon). I ordered a large mojito with boba and it was really good. It is something other boba shops in SGV don‚Äôt have. It‚Äôs refreshing, perfectly sweetened and divine. The concatenated boba pearl was chewy, warm and soft just the way I like it. Prices were inexpensive and very competitive. They have regular and large size containers. Furthermore, it has positive and motivating message at the back of every containers. Staff was nice and assiduous. Overall I HIGHLY recommend Hello Boba and will definitely try their other boba.</Review>

<text>We did a local move over a 3 day period of work.  The first day the crew was outstanding.  Really exceptional work.  Polite, hard working and friendly.  Day 2 was unloading day and we did discover after a week that things we had clearly labeled one room ended up in another.  Maybe < 5% of items.  Not a big deal in my mind.  We had worked out a color coding system with stickers and explained it to the team so it was just an honest mistake.  By the end of day 2 we felt like there was still a lot of work to do and we re-worked the quote for an addition 8-10 hours of work.  What I liked about Luke and his team is that they understood their initial estimate of time and materials was "off" and they worked with us on a final payment that seemed equitable to all.  The third day of work was difficult one because it all had to be done in one day and so the crew worked an extra long day until 10PM.  They should all be commended for staying late to get the job done.  The only thing that kept me from giving 5 stars was that I thought they could have done a better job estimating for a move that was local (only 4 miles away) and the way that they packed our Sleep Number Bed resulted in a lot of extra work for them and for us on the other end.  Besides those two things I would recommend this team to others and I would just say to make sure you take the time to do a proper estimate.<//text>< response>

So I did the research before buying a vehicle and got it down to a short list of 6-7 options. The focus was on Hyundai Santa Fe's available in CA. All of them 2018s, under $20k, and under 20k miles.

Most of them were located in SoCal but one was closer to home in Sacramento. Talked to the staff in Stockton and they had the vehicle transferred to their dealership, which saved me driving further.

Then I organised a one-way rental from a local Enterprise branch, headed up to Stockton and made the purchase. The staff were courteous, informative and helpful. Happy with the way things went and we were back on the road, in a little over an hour on our way home.

Financing went smoothly and the options were explained in detail so we able to decide on what we did and didn't need or want. I would highlight Enterprise ex-rentals to anyone looking for a late model car at a reasonable price with a good warranty package, (for Hyundais anyway).

I'd also point to doing your homework before you get to the purchasing stage of the process. I was totally stoked with our buy and wouldn't hesitate to recommend Enterprise sales as an option when buying your next car.</text>

<Text>Another nice outing at Carney's on the Strip. I enjoy eating outside on a sunny day, their outdoor area is very nice and relaxing,it has a great view of the strip, of the cool Art Deco Sunset Tower building. I enjoy eating there and watch the "action" , see what's going on the strip, people watch.

Food is as good as usual. Their beer menu has changed. An IPA is on tap now, Blue Moon instead of Sam Adams. I prefer a Sam Adams, but a Blue Moon still works with my New Yorker. My husband got his Chili dog as usual and we enjoyed a couple of large portion of fries. Splurge a tad, right? Since prices are reasonable here, this could be a fun, cheap date. Love the decor, the old train is unique, has a romantic vibe. Cool landmark of our city!<//Text><pics>None</pics><Response>None< /Response>< GmapID>

<Time>1531363939927<//Time><username>Larry Hollander< /username>< response>

<Rate>3<//Rate>< Review>
After reading all of the reviews on this nearby place I decided to give them a try.  Some of the reviews are either fake or extremely mean spirited people.  The place is reasonably clean.  The service was courteous and efficient.  The food was served quickly, 5 minutes to my table after ordering.  I had the tri tip platter with corn bread, and Mac & Cheese.  The tri tip was well cooked and very tender and tasty.  The Mac & Cheese tasted homemade not from a box.  I ordered a side of onion rings which were a bit greasy but tasty and also appeared to be homemade.

Was this the best BBQ I ever had?  No.  Was it the worst, far from it.  It is a small, appears to be family owned place that is trying to make a go of it in overtaxed, over charged rents, and over regulated California.  Give them a break!  I will return, it was tasty and satisfied my BBQ craving tonight.  I wish people would consider the families, employees and the owners of these small places before leaving harsh and mean spirited reviews that are not called for.<//Review>

<rate>2<//rate>< review>
One of my worst dining experiences ever!
TERRIBLE SERVICE / POOR FOOD QUALITY!

I stumbled across this place. It looked inviting and the menu featured a lot of creative options. There was a lunch special, so I thought I would give it a try.

What a mistake!

The cashier informed me there was a 15 minute wait to receive my take-away order. After checking-in on the order multiple times, it actually took them 45 minutes to prepare a simple chicken wrap with a side of hush puppies!

By the time I got the food, I was so hungry I ate pretty quickly.

It turns out that there was a 1/2-inch long, relatively thick chicken bone in the wrap! I almost chocked on it!

The staff here do not seem to put the necessary effort in for customer service and careful preparation of the food.

It's a shame, this place could be really cool if they worked on managing their operations.

The food tasted "alright".. (nothing worth coming back for), but obviously the service and poor food quality (chicken bones still in the meat) are enough reason to avoid this place!< /review>

<text>Don't come here unless you want your car to be held together by zip ties.

I brought my car in to have the brakes replaced as well as a few other routine things.  Everything seemed okay at first but then a couple days later as I was driving home from work my car started making a terribly loud flapping sound.  In disbelief that my car had finally grown wings to skip the traffic, I pulled over to find out the real cause of the noise.  Turns out that when my car was being fixed, they didn't put all the screws back in to the bottom of the front bumper that holds the engine splash shield in place.  There were supposed to be around 10-15 screws that hold it in place but there were only 3 screws.  So the flapping noise was the engine splash shield flapping around.  Because I'm a full time student with a full time job, I didn't have time to go back to the dealer right away, so I used duct tape to attach the engine splash shield to the bottom of the bumper.   I called the service manager and he didn't answer so I left a voicemail explaining the situation and that I wanted it fixed.  The service manager never called me back.

After a couple days, the duct tape came off while I was on the freeway and the engine splash shield started dragging on the ground.  The plastic is now worn down past where the holes were for the screws (that never got put back in my car at the dealership).  So that means that I need to get a new engine splash shield.  Apparently that's what you get when you spend several thousand dollars to get your car fixed.

Since the duct tape didn't work out too well, I'm now left with obnoxious bright blue zip ties sticking out of the front grill of my car just so that the engine splash shield doesn't drag on the ground.

Moral of the story: come here and within a week your car will be held together with zip ties.</text><time>1497661965504< /time>< pics>

<Text>Do not normally write these but I could not be more dissatisfied and will absolutely not be doing business here again for the following reasons:

1. In my first lease negotiations we came to an agreement on a price for a 2013 G37 Journey with no extra features; however, the only car they had in the color I wanted had some extra features I did not want but would settle for including in the depreciable base of the car in exchange for the color I like (foot plates, spare tire, etc. ~$800 total). When I got the deal for the new car, they kept the residual the same on the new car w/ extra features (which obviously had a higher cost basis), effectively passing 100% of the costs of those extra features on into my lease payments for things I didn't want. I ultimately caught the change in deals and resolved with Finance Manager the next day (good thing I decided to sleep on the deal). Probably wouldn't have caught that if I wasn't an accountant.
2. When I ultimately traded in said car towards the end of my lease term (started a new lease on an Infiniti Q50), they forgot to file some paperwork which they mailed to me the next day to sign. Not bad but pretty unprofessional allowing me to leave with the new vehicle without having signed all documents.
3. Accidentally left my garage door opener in the old car, called them the next day to grab it before the car was sold. Never heard back, reached out multiple times, garage door opener is gone.
3. Needed inspection info from the old car for tax purposes a couple months after the trade. Took me over a month and a half to receive the info from the Sales Associate from my initial request after a handful of voicemails, calls, texts, etc. Finally got the info in time to file my taxes (barely).
4. Latest issue (still ongoing): Got a failure to register notification from the DMV related to my old vehicle which I traded in months before I had to renew my registration. Long story short they need to notify the DMV of the transfer of title at the time of the trade which they never did and I have now called them on 6 different occasions each time, requesting someone keep me up to date on the status and have never once received a correspondence from them. The DMV issue is still not resolved, and the outstanding late fee is in risk of going to collections.

Overall, Infiniti is the best brand out there but this sales office is, in my opinion, completely pathetic when it comes to anything customer-service related. Once they put the keys in your hands (after they attempt to swindle you) all customer service is out the window. Proceed with caution.

Note to Perry Infiniti: FILE MY DMV PAPERWORK AND I WILL TAKE THIS POST DOWN. I AM DONE FOLLOWING UP ON THIS.

Regards,</Text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< resp>
